For those who donâ€™t really understand some of the story, basically the guy you see in this video is named Flint, who is passionate about creating art with graffiti, and is very good at what he does.   He comes across a box in an alleyway with an adorable living orb creature. It is a very happy creature, and its special power is bringing its happiness to anyone that encounters it. The little orb physically passes through Flintâ€™s heart, and he is brought an extreme amount of power, providing a new feeling of euphoria heâ€™s never experienced before.   He drops everything he is doing to spend all his time with the orb, so that he can receive more of its power. However even after all these positive feelings, Flint finds himself in an extremely depressive state, to the point where no matter what the magnitude of the orbâ€™s power, Flint cannot receive the same happiness that he was in the beginning.   He is exhausted, and eventually gets very angry for no reason, putting himself in immediate danger. On top of that, the orbâ€™s power starts to weaken, because it cannot bring its keeper any more joy. But it tries its best to pick Flint up. It gives him his paint spray can, of which he can create graffiti with, but he cannot bring himself to do it at all. Flint has lost his love for his craft, because of all the time he spent receiving power from the orb.   He is almost entirely decrepit, and he knows why. And so does the orb. So the orb disappears, and Flint is forced to let go. But in the end, his contentment, his passion, it all comes back to him, and he is once again free.

4GET is a song written about the crippling anxiety that I have always fought through in my life, either during or moving on from a relationship. I have a pattern of overthinking, and I feel like that hasnâ€™t ever changed. The feelings I go through in the middle of dating someone that Iâ€™m actively unsure about can be damaging, and I have to console with a counselor or friends in order to actively figure myself out. Iâ€™m unable to do the things that I love doing when Iâ€™m in this mindset that canâ€™t be truly cured until I end things with a potential partner. Iâ€™m working on that to this day. So I wanted to write this song for anyone that can relate, but in whatever way it speaks to them, not just to my specific situation. Many of us overthink, but maybe weâ€™ll forget about it. I created this song closely alongside The Living Tombstone. It was always a dream of mine to work with Yoav and Sam, and now Iâ€™m proud to call them my friends and close business partners. I brought OR3O on as well, because weâ€™ve worked together and been friends since I started out in my career. She is a wonderful singer, and Iâ€™m grateful for her participation on this important original song. The animation was created by a massive team of talented industry professionals. I came to a group of them to discuss the videoâ€™s concept, which I basically thought up right before we got into that meeting. They spent a year on this project, and I couldnâ€™t have done this without all of them. The story follows the protagonist, Flint, who is passionate about creating art with graffiti, and is very good at what he does. He comes across a box in an alleyway with an adorable living orb creature. It is a very happy creature, and its special power is bringing its happiness to anyone that encounters it. The little orb physically passes through Flintâ€™s heart, and he is brought an extreme amount of power, providing a new feeling of euphoria heâ€™s never experienced before. He drops everything he is doing to spend all his time with the orb, so that he can receive more of its power. Eventually, even after all these positive feelings, Flint finds himself in an extremely depressive state, to the point where no matter what the magnitude of the orbâ€™s power, Flint cannot receive the same happiness that he was in the beginning. He is exhausted, and eventually gets very angry for no reason, putting himself in immediate danger. On top of that, the orbâ€™s power starts to weaken, because it cannot bring its keeper any more joy. But it tries its best to pick Flint up. It gives him his paint spray can, of which he can create graffiti with, but he cannot bring himself to do it at all. Flint has lost his love for his craft, because of all the time he spent receiving power from the orb. He is almost entirely decrepit, and he knows why. And so does the orb. So the orb disappears, and Flint is forced to let go. But in the end, his contentment, his passion, it all comes back to him, and he is once again free. This story came so easily to me, because those feelings and experiences were very fresh to me at the time of coming up with it. I was going through a breakup that needed to happen for my own good. In the midst of the relationship, I knew that it wasnâ€™t right for me, and it wasnâ€™t fair to them. But I felt like I wanted to keep trying, and I wanted to hold onto the experience. But I was depressed, very anxious, and I hurt the both of us very deeply in the process. It took a very long time, but I came out of it feeling better and more hopeful for a brighter future. That doesnâ€™t mean the pain and anxiety I feel is all over for me. But Iâ€™m learning about myself, and Iâ€™m learning to live a happier life, one song at a time.

Coming back to this a year after feels kinda nostalgic..
This song dropped at a point in my life when I was ready to die. Throughout the entirety of 2023 I was depressed to the point of attempting several times. This song was exactly my mental state at that time, I didn't feel like I could control my own mind and I was in the passenger seat but still trying to make the best of it. I used to listen to this song on loop back and forth to my psych appointments and even during the very few times I was okay during that year I listened to this song. It all came to a head when I was institutionalized on the 10th of October. I'm not okay, but I'm doing much better now. This song for that reason will hold a special place in my heart, not for making sure I was good, but making sure I was okay.

Man i cried
This story, just in the story of the song itself, is interesting. A graffiti artist comes across a ball of happiness that brings him a feeling of happiness, of contentedness, which ends up fading over time because he had grown reliant on the orb, tossing away the craft that was the backbone of the happiness, in the end, the orb begins to break down into dust, and for once, it seems melancholic, but it manages one last smile, which brought to light the craft that our protagonist had forgotten their enjoyment of.  And then there's the story behind the story of the song. I listened to the song the first time, and nearly wept, not because I felt an overarching story behind it, but because I related to it more than I liked to admit. I went through a rough patch in my own hobby, I like to write, but I found myself writing less and less because it felt so taxing, so draining on my creativity, and it felt like everything I liked about my work was all the things I had to draw inspiration to write. I felt like quitting, stopping myself from continuing to try, and for a while, I did stop, even now, I've yet to fully start back up, I write to kill time, but I don't apply myself fully to it anymore, it's more of an idle thing, much like humming. For those people who too feel trapped to a cycle of doing something you enjoy only to start not enjoying it much anymore, you aren't alone, many people go through the rough patches, and you shouldn't give up, it will get better!  TL;DR: personal experiences with depressing things led me to learn that if you enjoy something, keep going, and no matter what, you'll find your perfect balance, and you can get through it

Do not understand what it is
here's my analysis of this song: (read the story behind this song too, it's in the desc)  "moving on, moving on, it doesnt really matter, my brain follows a pattern, forget about it" this probably means that people with anxiety often feel like they dont matter, and they should just forget about it. the brain always overthinks but we keep telling ourselves to stop, and forget  "breaking up, breaking down, you think that it'll get better but it never does"  with anxiety, you avoid things that make you anxious, and hope it'll just magically disappear, but it's just avoiding it instead of confronting, which is very scary to do  "i feel like im dying" probably states the feeling of having a panic attack. it feels like you're about to pass out or die. your heart beats fast, ears ringing, hyperventilating. it's a very scary experience.  "nobody tells me i'm lying. couldnt hear when i was crying" i think it means that most anxiety goes unnoticed. with anxiety, you often fear what people will think of you and your emotions, and  you often hide it and no one can see your suffering. also why the music in this song is very happy, whereas the lyrics are about charlie's experience with crippling anxiety. it's about hiding the suffering  "it's defeating when i'm trying to forget about it" trying to forget about anxiety and fear is a very hard and mentally taxing thing to do. every time you try to forget about your anxious feelings, the more it comes to haunt you  "all the silence getting louder" it's a feeling that i cant really describe. you kinda have to experience it to find out. but it is not a pleasant experience.  "Iâ€™m spending every day, Wishing I was okay. Surrendered to a world of gray." this is more about depression. again, not sure how to explain this one, but the lyrics kind of explain itself i guess? but the gray part, it's like the world is desaturated. food doesnt taste as good, things arent that enjoyable anymore, and yeah, you get the deal.  "My car is broken down, I canâ€™t get out of town." it's describing a feeling of being stuck at a point in life.  "All my thoughts are getting scattered. Am I madder than a hatter?" with a ton of overthinking, you can easily feel like you're going insane.  as for the last scene, flint tries to get back into his old hobby, but with anxiety and depression, it gets quite scary to do it. it is seen that flint is forced to let go of the orb, creating separation anxiety, grief and/or withdrawal.

I've been so close to reaching out yet never do because the thought is so scary. But as other comments I've seen have said, healing is definitely a journey and everyone is on their own journey. You are one of those singers that I associate only in a positive way and always cheer me up with your songs. Regarding the video and its idea, I want to share my experience. I was in apathy for almost a year and a half, but only recently everything began to improve. I was lost, I felt the shame of the past every day, as well as the inability to return to the good old days. Lack of confidence in myself and the future, I constantly asked myself: "What am I living for? What is my goal as a person, and not as an animal?" All this is very familiar to me... Guys, all those who are also among you in the same condition as I have been for these half a year, I want to tell you, in no case do not despair. Life is changeable, it has ups and downs, and that's okay. I realized for myself: "The night is not endless, the sun will always rise above you." Based on this statement, I want to say, no matter how bad you feel, never give up. It will be difficult, but only through tears, suffering, etc., when your personal dawn comes, you will understand that all this was not in vain. Play sports and do what you like. Amogus 0:03
I love the song bro
I feel this so hard.  It reminds me of my journey with art from my elementary school years to adult hood mainly the start and near the end of this.  First off I have adhd and anxiety. Both of these affected my journey threw this.  Art was my go to way to forget about this world. I drawed my little pony despite people making fun of me of drawing ponies I had a small group that all though left me eventually I drawed small mlp comics that was pretty simple and not a big deal.  Once I got into high-school I took a break from ponies at that time and drawed my oc way more. Her name is rocky, I had for awhile starting out as EnderRocky and evolving into something new. With new ocs around her.  But then.. comes in the art teacher there.. all my love towards art came crashing and was destroyed by her. It gets worse when some say she helped them. Because she seemed to had favorites someone I assume she deems talented or acts correctly gets to have breaks, play games, and such even if their behind a project.  As for me I got jumped for playing yugioh when I was done drawing. She demanded I draw instead but i couldn't bring myself to draw without a idea it was already bad enough I had projects from her. She was lucky I try to figure out ways for myself to do that.   Her teaching is the worse I've ever seen in a teacher. We were stuck on shading for half of the semester and because of it I hate pencil shading now. If you saw my projects from then you can tell how badly it was effecting me. All though lost I still remember the first and final one. The first was a sphere and people can see I done it before and was good at it. But the final project it look like I wasn't good at shading some look nice other parts didn't. I was so tired of doing it.  Then all the other projects we only got 1 practice or she make us watch something then stright to the main project. It was horrible. Once I finally graduated I didn't draw for a year and a half that much only once or twice. Combine that with the death of my grandpa I couldn't ever draw.  Eventually I finally grab that art tablet I got from saving spare change months ago from my grandpa and dad paid what was left. I slowly tried to draw and figure out something I may enjoy doing digitally.   I went back, back to ponies. I did lineless with a fur effect and loved it. Eventually I found a brush I liked for lines and used that not only that but I realize this brush can make a effect with my coloring and I though it look real nice. Shading was the hardest part to figure out for me on my art I ended up going with a watercolor brush. Last night before this i went on a drawing spree, I drawed rocky again it came out much better then I ever did in the past. Then I drawed another oc. I end the night with a half finished "draw the squad" meme I was doing for the giggles.   I love the way I do things now, I don't care if it takes longer then normal for most people I love how the art turns out. This video makes me feel like I'm on that journey again for a moment, specially with the character being a artiest at first but lost it.

This the real story about the story: (btw you should read the full document about this, is in the description!)  The story follows the protagonist, Flint, who is passionate about creating art with graffiti, and is very good at what he does. He comes across a box in an alleyway with an adorable living orb creature. It is a very happy creature, and its special power is bringing its happiness to anyone that encounters it. The little orb physically passes through Flintâ€™s heart, and he is brought an extreme amount of power, providing a new feeling of euphoria heâ€™s never experienced before. He drops everything he is doing to spend all his time with the orb, so that he can receive more of its power.   Eventually, even after all these positive feelings, Flint finds himself in an extremely depressive state, to the point where no matter what the magnitude of the orbâ€™s power, Flint cannot receive the same happiness that he was in the beginning. He is exhausted, and eventually gets very angry for no reason, putting himself in immediate danger.   On top of that, the orbâ€™s power starts to weaken, because it cannot bring its keeper any more joy. But it tries its best to pick Flint up. It gives him his paint spray can, of which he can create graffiti with, but he cannot bring himself to do it at all. Flint has lost his love for his craft, because of all the time he spent receiving power from the orb. He is almost entirely decrepit, and he knows why. And so does the orb. So the orb disappears, and Flint is forced to let go. But in the end, his contentment, his passion, it all comes back to him, and he is once again free.

I genuinely relate to this HELL of a banger CG5, OR3O, and The Living Tombstone made, for I have some type of anxiety (like Flint). In life lies multiple barriers to break, thin or thick. Sometimes these barriers can feel like generations to break through off, "[surrounding people] in a world of gray/grey" (1:08 - OR3O). Motivation can die out, "silence can grow louder", meanwhile vibrant colors ranging from life can fade, as if people can't feel the need to push through, causing life to be dull and helpless. It's crazy how anxiety can do many harmful things that can hurt humanity NOT just physically, but also mentally. Anxiety can push you from others, bury away your emotions, lose motivation in what you love to do, focus on one thing more than the other, worry about what the future can hold, AND hundreds, thousands, or even BILLIONS of other twisted things. For instance, right now I am struggling to pursue my motivation to do things I adore doing (these interests make me who I REALLY am in my identity). I have lost motivation ever since 2021/2022, and it's been a year since I've genuinely made some content on my main channel because I push myself to do more school than animating. As I do more school, anxiety grew around the corner. I am frightened if I won't ever gain motivation to animate, and more things again on my channel; because I DREAM to be a YouTube Star, and an inspiration to many. I know I have pretty decent animation skills, but I just don't know what content to make, and I fear I may fail in school. For I am currently a thirteen year old, apprehensive about what the future holds. It's just like every step I make, more school work piles in, and I barely get any breaks in it. Weekends feel short, weekdays feel long, my barrier just has a scratch. I just don't know what to do. However, in my soul, lies a little bit of determination and light. Everytime I'm at my lowest times, I suddenly just feel a shine of hope. Oh, and everytime I feel hope, trust me-- it's such motivational feeling. Although my "thoughts are feeling scattered" , I just remember my inspirations, and loved ones who can help me break my barrier of anxiety. And to those who have anxiety, you can break it too. I believe everyone who has anxiety can too break the thickest barrier they have one day. Yes, there may be hardships; but just remember there are multiple individuals who can help you continue on, inspirations OR loved ones.   Life is not made to be wasted because of anxiety, Life is used to become want you dream to be, to cherish moments with those who you love, to spend. ğŸ’™  BUT, getting that out of the way, this is a catchy melody! 10/10, and bravo! Nate and Fadey started to have fun.  Until Nate nearly got ran over by a car.  When Nate looked at Fadey, part of him was missing. The end.  Hope you like the story version! My interpretation of the song and visuals:  A graffiti artist is living their normal life. Eat, sleep, art, repeat. One day, they start hearing a whispering voice invading their mind. Sometimes it's happy, sometimes it makes them 4get things, and sometimes it's sad. This voice slowly becomes more and more real with each passing day, making the person forget a lot of things and feel emotions they don't usually feel. The voice also makes the person feel 'grey' at times (surrounded by a world of grey). As the artist slowly becomes more and more disconnected from their normal life, the voice grows louder. They try to avoid it, hence all the running scenes and the almost-accident scene, when they reach a dead end - their old painting spot. The art soothes the voice as it grows fainter and fainter, finally going away. The artist realizes that art saved them, as they establish a new relationship with their art and roots and finally leads a normal life again. Tell me what you think! It's interesting to see the guy's hair change from vivid brown to gray as it seems that they enter a deeper depressive state. As if the color drains from their hair as their desire to art falls away slowly. Then the little light, a little ball of hope that follows him around as a physical reminder of his past desire that looms around him and as he tries more and more things, it just becomes more apparent that it won't go away, no matter how hard he tries to do something else and "forget about it".   The day being high value colors and filled with life, as the time of his life where everything is lively and colorful. Then, as he finds art as his passion, his little ball of hope, he looks around and finds fault in his own work compared to everything around. Filling his mind with senseless noise to deter him, he tries to forget about the passion in the hopes he won't fall victim to comparing himself to everything. Trying new things doesn't seem to help him any as he fails in them, then he goes and finds his passion for art playing around with everything around him, at the theaters and in the park, reminding him of his passion. As night comes, there is no life around and the low value colors darken his life. The only light remaining is his little ball of hope and passion for art that keeps him going through the dark times, which he vehemently tries to fight and get away from for fear his passion would not being good enough. Then he gets shocked by a life-altering event in the darkness that leaves him to realize that there is no good or bad and he needs to turn his life around. However, due to his constant fighting his passion, he starts to lose himself as his passion finally starts to slip away in front of his own eyes. As he rushes through the dark, he finds himself back where he once found his passion for art, from where it all began. As he tries to rush into art to keep his little hope alive, he can't find it within himself to do so as there is no more fuel for that small passion and it disappears. As he is enveloped in the darkness, as he doesn't create something immediately, he remembers that he can't just give up and forget again. Slowly, realization shines on him, and it is bigger than ever as he finally comes to see his passion as something that isn't small and weak. His passion is bright and will light up the dark times as he stops forgetting and remembers that he doesn't have to be the biggest out there nor the best. Just that it makes him happy to do it.  At least, that's my take on the whole shebang. I love it to bits and will be listening to it for quite some time to come. Thank y'all for this masterpiece.
